mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省新乡市原阳县基督教牧师。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">近年来，因反对中共当局强拆十字架，拒绝把教堂内“爱神爱人”标语改成“爱国爱教”及在教堂内建国旗台，随遭河南省当局打压逼迫；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被新乡市原阳县警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑事拘留，另有三名教会同工（即神职工作人员）亦被抓捕，随后几日，其所在中心堂十字架迅速被当地宗教局、公安局及城管等多个部门联合强拆，教堂内“爱神爱人”等标语被清除，教堂内被强行竖立起五星红旗；一个多月后，被抓三名同工均获取保候审，而其却被一直羁押不放，后被原阳县检察院正式批捕，指控其涉嫌“职务侵占、妨害公务和销毁账目”；截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其案件已在两度退回公安局补充侦查后，再次移送检察院，进入审查起诉阶段；据悉，其儿子称，当局对其父亲的一切指控均属莫须有罪名，旨在对其拒绝与官方合作态度进行刻意“打击报复”。目前被羁押于新乡市原阳县看守所（河南省新乡市原阳县葛埠口乡丘庙村，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">453500</span>。）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李俊华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。李俊华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李俊伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，李俊伟在天津街讲真相被吉林市昌邑区派出所与国保大队警察抓捕，在拘留所非法拘留七天后，又送入吉林市看守所关押迫害。李俊伟被关押一年后获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李霖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆乌鲁木齐公民李霖因言获罪<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被新疆警方刑事拘留。原因是其曾在海外的推特上发推批评新疆当局的政策，新疆警方先是以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”对其逮捕，后李霖遭控“煽动颠覆国家政权”，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李龙全：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1963</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，贵州省毕节市纳雍县人，又名李老五，中国在押维权人士。因长期未得到政府赔付的足额退耕还林补偿，索要遭拒，故而多次上访；曾因揭露当地政府为征地进行暗箱操作，不仅拒付村民合理补偿而且还打残村民，其本人亦遭殴打，肠子被打漏；其被迫无奈走上漫长艰难的维权之路；然上访几年，倾家荡产而无果；曾因和多个维权访民到当地王家寨政府及县政府门口拉横幅上访投诉，使得地方执政者十分不满；省委第九巡视组进驻纳雍县时，曾因到巡视组住地要求与巡视组人员见面，表达合理诉求，不得见，便拉幅喊冤，抗议政府强征、暴力执法及三条命案，遂遭到地方当局的严厉打压和疯狂报复；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因其和<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名维权访民一同欲赴京上访，反映全村<span lang="EN-US">970</span>亩退耕还林土地款被县政府非法扣留事宜，不料被访民中的政府内线告发，其一行<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余人在贵州省水城黄土坡“新雨旅社”集合时，被赶来的纳雍县警方随即抓捕，其中除有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多人跑掉之外，剩下<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被悉数拘留，后虽放出<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人，但其却被一直被刑拘于纳雍县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被纳雍县检察院以涉嫌“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，控其因组织村民在当地政府门口，用拉横幅、喊口号及游行等方式表达诉求，并将抗议过程拍摄、发布到“六四天网”，因此触犯了有关法律，属于违法行为；据悉，其儿子曾去派出所询问父亲为何被捕，竟遭警方殴打并被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年某日，被贵州省纳雍县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，经贵州省毕节市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。目前疑在贵州省都匀监狱（贵州省黔南布依族苗族自治州都匀市羊场街<span lang="EN-US">26</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">558000</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李梅花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李梅花与李淑东、彭正花：女，云南省昭通市基督徒、教会传道人，良心犯。因从事基督教家庭教会敬拜及讲道传教活动而遭到云南省当局的所谓专项整治严打，被污名化为在当地从事“三班仆人派”邪教组织活动。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被临沧、楚雄、昭通、大理等市警方分别抓捕刑拘。其中，李淑东、李梅花、彭正花等多人于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被昭通市警方以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式逮捕，被指控三人“组织信徒非法集会从事邪教活动，制作、传播邪教宣传品，破坏了国家法律、行政法规的实施、扰乱社会秩序危害社会的行为，已构成组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日其一行多人分别被昭通市法院以同罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，其中李淑东、李梅花、彭正花三人各被一审判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。三人均不服判决，已提出上诉。据称，法官对此态度很糟糕。目前她们都被关押在昭通市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李美化<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省咸阳市礼泉县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，陕西省柞水县公安局国保大队郭淑琴带领公安、武警几十人全副武装，荷枪实弹，跑了几百里路，包围了李美化家所在村的一条街道，抢走了她家私人财物达三、四万元之多，同时抓捕了李美化到柞水县看守所。李美化的丈夫袁玉龙当时走脱。最后夫妻二人袁玉龙被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年和李美化被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。李美化刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李明书：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州省桐梓县燎原镇花园村年近古稀的村民李明书，因与其他村民举报原镇长王国燕、村支书令狐昌华、杨小勇、国土所长易正芳在征地拆迁中，徇私枉法、以权谋私、中饱私囊，侵犯村民的利益，在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午在贵阳机场被抓捕，在被刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天后被正式逮捕。李明书在看守所换仓后受到牢头狱霸的威胁，要其赶快认罪，不然，就要拳头伺候。家人要求给父亲送冬天的帽子不被允许。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李明哲</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，祖籍安徽省人，实为中华民国台北市人，前台湾立委许钟碧霞国会办公室助理，前台北市议员谢明达竞选总部助选员，台湾民主进步党党员，非政府组织“人权公约施行监督联盟”<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>志工，首个被中国大陆公审的台湾人，人权活动者。早期曾参加台湾新党青年军，并在大学期间因受自由思潮启蒙，与现任妻子李净瑜共同参与反对台湾高学费运动。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年曾先后任台湾民主进步党社会发展部专员和前新台湾文化基金会专员。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月曾担任非政府组织“人权公约施行监督联盟”志工。多年来，曾因长期关注中国人权状况及民主维权运动等议题，尤其是基于大陆许多人有阅读人权、近代史、政党选举等书籍的需要，自费邮赠大量文学与社科类书籍，而一直受到中共当局的严密监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月曾因邮寄台湾书籍而遭到中共当局的查扣没收。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日当其前往中国大陆，途径澳门关卡再转入境到珠海拱北口岸时，被莫名消失，其妻及社会各界频繁呼吁亦无消息，直至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才从中国官方获悉，其被国家安全部以涉“危害国家安全”罪由拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被湖南省检察院以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕，被控其“自<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年以来，频繁进入大陆活动，与大陆有关人员勾结，制定行动纲领，建立非法组织，策划、实施颠覆我国家政权的活动”，属违法犯罪行为。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其案在岳阳市中级法院开庭受审，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被该法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前被羁押于湖南省岳阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李南海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">他与邓洪成、肖兵、王军、沈力、丁岩、王威、王建华、黄安阳、李江鹏等广东深圳公民<span lang="EN-US">10</span>公民遭抓捕。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">以上<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日后连续遭拘捕或强迫失踪。后警方向追寻下落的邓洪成、王军家属证实其已被羁押，被指涉颠覆。后被告知指定居所监视居住。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李润芳：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">46</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，女，山西省太原市杏花岭区人，残疾人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。曾因信仰和练习法轮功遭<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年冤狱迫害。出狱后多次到杏花岭区涧河派出所办理身份证，竟被非法拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日再次去办理身份证时被太原市杏花岭区警方随即扣留、刑拘，后被以涉嫌邪教罪正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日再次被太原市杏花岭区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半；李润芳不服，已提出上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李珊珊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津法轮功学员周向阳妻子。李珊珊因坚持为在<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年丈夫周向阳申冤，曾遭到监狱的报复，两次被非法劳教共计三年多。二零一三年劳教制度解体了，李珊珊是从石家庄女子劳教所走出来的最后一个。一家人团聚的日子没有多久。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日早晨七点，天津警察再一次破门而入，把周向阳和妻子李珊珊抓走了。周向阳被判七年，李珊珊被判六年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李绍志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十四岁，原为佳木斯市煤矿机械厂工人。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日去北京为法轮功上访被抓捕，后劳教一年。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日李绍志和其他十一名法轮功学员不堪忍受劳教所的虐待，逃离劳教所，从此被迫流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，李绍志回到家乡佳木斯，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被举报抓捕，后被判刑五年，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出狱。之后去了哈尔滨，在哈尔滨多年来靠打工维持生活。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，租住在哈尔滨南岗区的李绍志，被长春市南关区民康派出所警察，协同哈尔滨市警察在他租住的楼前抓捕。被关押在长春市第三看守所。长春市南关区法院<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日对法轮功学员李绍志开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李生金</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：青海省大通县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被青海省大通县警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被青海省大通县法院一审以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李淑东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李淑东、李梅花、彭正花：女，云南省昭通市基督徒、教会传道人，良心犯。因从事基督教家庭教会敬拜及讲道传教活动而遭到云南省当局的所谓专项整治严打，被污名化为在当地从事“三班仆人派”邪教组织活动。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被临沧、楚雄、昭通、大理等市警方分别抓捕刑拘。其中，李淑东、李梅花、彭正花等多人于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被昭通市警方以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式逮捕，被指控三人“组织信徒非法集会从事邪教活动，制作、传播邪教宣传品，破坏了国家法律、行政法规的实施、扰乱社会秩序危害社会的行为，已构成组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日其一行多人分别被昭通市法院以同罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，其中李淑东、李梅花、彭正花三人各被一审判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。三人均不服判决，已提出上诉。据称，法官对此态度很糟糕。目前她们都被关押在昭通市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李树南：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，湖北省荆州市监利县白螺镇人，监利县白螺镇五里庙村村民，司法不公举报人，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，曾因承包邻村彭阮村<span lang="EN-US">110</span>亩土地搞多种养殖期间，当地监利县柘木乡政府官员非法平整土地致其岳母家农田出现严重损毁现象，其协助家人被迫向上反映，以求妥善解决问题，孰料多次投诉无果，反起冲突、被造假；后其逐渐认识到投诉无门，上访反被造假诬告皆因地方官员相互勾结贪污公款（即：以县委书记为首勾结乡村干部做假帐截留救灾资金，倒卖救灾物资，贪污工程青苗补偿款），坑害百姓所致，至此开始逐级上访；曾因其举报维权触动了地方官员的私利（即采用重复申报水利工程项目等诈骗国家资金），而遭当局强力逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，其曾遭报复性殴打，致其身体终生残疾；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因其夫妻二人承包的鱼塘在地方干部的纵容下被人破坏，承包合同被单方废止，而使其直接经济损失多达<span lang="EN-US">60</span>余万元；曾因其妻陈呈香出于义愤，采取极端抗议方式点火自焚，以求正义公道，其为此提起上诉，但在同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日信访投诉听证会上却因地方当局提供伪证，其夫妇二人被警方分别行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因其妻两次进京投诉而被监利县警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共秩序罪”刑拘，后又被宣布劳动教养，至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日才被释放，故而其维权抗争之心日益弥坚；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在京信访反映冤情时遭到北京警方地毯式抓铺，后被移交给监利县截访人员遣返原籍，又被关进某宾馆式黑监狱，遭到群殴，致其身体多处受伤；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被荆州市监利县警方从家中突然带走，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，知其早已被转正式批捕，其案现已被检察院以同罪由移交至湖北省荆州市监利县法院；未审待判。目前被羁押于荆州市监利县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李天学：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。李天学刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李铁：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1959</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日出生，湖北省武汉市人，笔名：华汉武，九鼎煲汤，网络作家，异议人士，中国在押政治犯。曾多次撰写文章在网上发表，以期推动民主、宪政国家和直接地方选举，并积极参与深圳等地的维护公民宪法权利活动，多次参与发起在苏州举行的网友公祭林昭活动。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年当其再次前往苏州参加公祭林昭活动的过程中，<span lang="EN-US"> 9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被武汉警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US"> 10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被武汉市检察院以同罪名批捕，理由是他在网络上发表了《人以尊严为天》等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>篇文章，其目的是“以民主的名义，达到推翻国家政权、和平演变”，其具体行为表现是“参加三至五人集会、加入中国社会民主党党派，和敌对势力的网站联系”；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被武汉市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前在湖北省黄岗市陆口镇鄂东监狱服刑；据悉，其在狱中患有高血压，且一直受到官方严格限制，既不可与外界打电话、写信，又不可会见除直系亲属之外的其他亲属，其女儿、母亲每次探监仅准见面<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李薇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省长春市人，法轮功信仰者、良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月在广西壮族自治区阳朔县发放破网（又称“翻墙”）软件光盘时，被阳朔县警方绑架，后被以涉“邪教罪”刑拘、逮捕。广西阳朔县法院先后对其于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日两次予以庭审，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日终被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，刑期至于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李伟涛：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，辽阳法轮功学员李伟涛、王永生、国世游、谷林杰、汤显贺、罗丽被辽阳市白塔公安分局国保警察马文博等人绑架、抄家，当时国世游身体不适被多个警察抬着抓走的。辽宁省辽阳市白塔区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月对李伟涛等六名法轮功学员判刑，刑期是：李伟涛<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王永生<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罗丽<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、汤显贺<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、国世游<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、谷林杰<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并附带罚款，其中五人已上诉。李伟涛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李文德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河南省商丘市民权县人，商丘市民权县双塔乡韭菜里村农民，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日曾因信仰、维护法轮功而被河南省地方当局处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。获释后，因坚持信仰自由并继续宣传法轮功真相，而于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年又被地方当局以涉邪教罪名义处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，关押于河南省许昌市劳教所；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年秋，曾因与多人一起去商丘市民权县野鸡岗乡宣传法轮功，而被民权县警方刑拘、逮捕，后被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并被关押于河南省新密市新密监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年出狱后，因控诉前中共国家领导人江泽民打压迫害法轮功成员，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被商丘民权县警方再次以涉“邪教罪”刑拘，关押于河南省睢县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月在不通知其家人的情况下被秘判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。据悉，因其多次被非法关押，其<span lang="EN-US">84</span>岁老母受到多次惊吓，已于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份去世。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李文明：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，甘肃省兰州市人，原名李明义、李明一，原甘肃省兰州机车厂职工，法轮功信仰者，原兰州市七里河法轮功辅导站负责人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因信仰和负责兰州七里河地区法轮功信仰者的管理工作，被当地警方从工作单位非法抓捕，至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月后才被释放；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，曾因前往北京上访，被北京警方非法关押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因参加被迫害致死的兰州法轮功信仰者姚宝荣的悼念，被警方当场非法绑架、劫持，后被送至兰州市平安台劳教所劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因其获释后又被强迫接受洗脑教育，其不堪受辱虐待而逃离洗脑班，随被警方悬赏通缉；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被兰州市七里河警方再次抓捕、刑拘，关押在兰州市第一看守所，后被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年；据悉，其在狱中遭受严重迫害，多次受恶徒殴打、电击等酷刑折磨，生命垂危，同时，因其自幼是孤儿，妻子肖彦红亦因信仰法轮功而被判刑，故迄今无人前往探视。目前在甘肃省兰州监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李希军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">她和张建兰是山东临沂高新区访民，系母女。临沂市公安局高新区技术产业开发区分局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出具的拘留通知书中显示，将张建兰以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，羁押在临沂市看守所。张建兰的亲属表示，张建兰的母亲李希军也被刑拘，和张建兰关押在一个看守所。但警方没给母亲的拘留通知书。其亲属表示，张建兰已经两个多月不上访了，在家照顾孙女，和刚刚生下来才十几天的小孙子，不知道为什么给拘留了。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李晓波：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，四川省人，前四川省仁寿县副书记、前四川省蒲江县县长，原某房产公司总经理，法轮功修炼者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年中共将法轮功定为“邪教”之后，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年遂被四川省成都市警方逮捕，并被当地法院以“邪教罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，关押于四川省德阳监狱，受尽摧残折磨，直至<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年才准予获释；出狱后，其信仰意志弥坚，继续进行法轮功修炼并传播法轮功真相，遂遭致当局的严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，因其在成都市龙泉驿区金堂县给村民散发法轮功真相传单，被当地洪安派出所警方强行抓走（注：当时被野蛮抓捕的还有其子李喆，后因李喆已是加拿大籍公民，遂被当局强行遣回加拿大）并被刑拘，其家被抄，且所有被抄物品包括四台计算机和打印机等，均不给开据任何没收清单；后被正式逮捕，超期关押于四川省成都市龙泉驿看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，终被四川省成都市龙泉驿法院再次以“利用邪教组织颠覆国家法律罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。目前在四川省德阳监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李先利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省合江县公民。李先利因在境外服务器创办网站“破楼梦”（<span lang="EN-US">http://polou.me</span>，现已注销），并在上面发表所谓“辱骂、丑化国家领导人、国家机关及国家机关工作人员、丑化党的基本制度的内容”，所以于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被四川合江县警方刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被四川省合江县人民法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。其不服判决，立即提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日经四川省泸州市中级人民法院二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判。理由是，李先利利用境外服务器开设网站“破楼梦”，从<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月起就先后发表了“从钉子户到部级邪教”、“书记奖金几条被”、“骨灰哪儿去了”、“稻谷仓<span lang="EN-US">8</span>号问题求解”、“<span lang="EN-US">250</span>元人民币漫画”、“泸州九狮山”打油诗、“中国备胎党”等多个文章及图片，由于内容大都涉及丑化、辱骂国家领导人、国家机关及其工作人员，丑化党的基本制度，严重损害了党和国家的形象，并且还通过<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信群，将“破楼梦”网站链接及相应内容、图片直接发给网络好友们分享，破坏了社会秩序，其行为已构成寻衅滋事罪。又因其有前科（李先利曾在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被合江县人民法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年），须从重处罚，所以二审裁决，依然维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李秀芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员，今年（<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年）<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日给营口市站前区东桥派出所、新兴派出所送政府相关文件时被警察非法扣押、构陷，被关押在营口市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日李秀芬遭站前区法院庭审。在法庭上，律师为她做了无罪辩护，李秀芬自己也认为自己无罪（她被非法关押在营口市看守所九个多月）。尽管如此，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月其家属从辩护律师处听说，李秀芬被辽宁省营口市站前区法院<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李雪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东胶州法轮功学员。一家人因信仰被迫害多年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，李雪及其母亲宋桂香通过快递分别向北京最高检察院、最高法院邮寄了刑事控告书，控告江泽民发起对法轮功学员的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，以阜安派出所负责人想找她们母女“谈话”的名义将宋桂香、李雪骗至派出所，然后羁押于青岛普东看守所进行迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，李雪被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年重刑，现在山东省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李学良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省北安市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日夜晚，马义涛等三名法轮功学员开车到五大连池市发放法轮功真相资料。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日凌晨，他们被跟踪的警察抓捕，同时被抓捕的法轮功学员还有李学良、盛春霞。随后警察驱车到北安市城区马义涛的家抄家，抢劫走几本大法著作和真相资料，并抓捕了马义涛的妻子马英杰。）<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，马义涛等四人被黑龙江省亚布力林区法院判刑。马义涛被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，李学良<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，马英杰<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，盛春霞判三年缓四年，已回家。马义涛、李学良不服法院非法判决，提出上诉。李学良刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 311.25pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李艳秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁锦州市太和区，法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十二岁。她修炼法轮功十多年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，李艳秋在向世人发送法轮功台历时，遭锦州太和区国保大队警察绑架，李艳秋家中的电脑、大法书籍等私人物品，被警察强行拿走。后她被关押到锦州市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午，锦州市太和区法院在不通知家属的情况下，在锦州看守所对李艳秋秘密开庭，法院指定了法律援助律师为她作有罪辩护，而李艳秋一直没有认过罪。法官在李艳秋身体极度虚弱、不能独立行走、不能完整表达意愿的情况下，匆匆走了过场。后获知李艳秋已经被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李奕哲</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：男，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生人，吉林人，北京师范大学毕业，北京电影学院博士研究生毕业。法轮功信众。捕前在江苏省南京市江宁大学城南广学院任教。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年底，被南京市公安局江宁分局，以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪，刑事拘留随后遭逮捕。现羁押在南京市江宁区看守所。他的妹妹也是法轮功信仰者，被判刑三年半，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月刚出狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李银秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东鹤山市沙坪街道浸信教会传道人梁子亮的妻子，梁子亮和李银秀<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日带领信徒在当地一公园内拉横幅反对堕胎以及传福音，当晚被警察传唤到派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，梁子亮与妻子李银秀的家属，接到鹤山市公安局发出的刑事拘留通知书，两份通知书分别指梁子梁和李银秀，违反刑事诉讼法第八十条之规定，涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集罪，刑事拘留，现羁押在鹤山市看守所。据信徒介绍，梁子亮原是当地官办三自教会的信徒，后离开“三自”，成立家庭教会。目前，浸信教会有信徒约二十人。每周举行聚会，梁子亮还会带领信徒外出传福音，也因此多次受到警察警告。广东省基督教因传福音被刑事拘留的案子，并不多见。很多教会担心当局此举是为了震慑其他家庭教会，以阻止信徒外出传福音。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李媛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，辽宁省沈阳市人，辽阳市朝光村基督教家庭教会骨干成员，中国在押良心犯。因其教会为基督教家庭教会，且不愿到中共当局指定的“三自”教会敬拜、聚会，遂遭致当局的严打惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被辽阳市太子河区警方突然抓捕刑拘，并被指控教会内部使用了基督徒信仰灵修崇拜书籍及相关印刷品，并在教会的便利店销往其他省市，属于非法买卖行为；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前被羁押于辽阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李玉方：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年已过<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，哈尔滨古稀老人、法轮功学员李玉方因善心向百姓传法轮功真相，遭抓捕。在她全不知晓的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，哈尔滨道外法院对老人秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，后将她送到哈尔滨女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李玉凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李玉凤：<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，河南省焦作市人，基督徒，维权公民。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末，曾因家中惨遭两次政府不当拆迁，损失巨大，其被迫提起诉讼，打赢了官司，但因被告是当地政府，法院不予执行，故而其被迫上访维权；曾因不断维权，被当局进行恶意打击报复，并以“妨害公务罪”对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；出狱后其继续状告地方政府，再遭逼迫，又被劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；两次入狱，备受酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日因与他人前往监狱迎接“新公民运动”维权代表袁冬出狱，并率先打出横幅“欢迎袁冬从小监狱回到大监狱”，又被北京大兴区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被北京市大兴区检察院批捕，至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被取保候审释放。关押期间，曾被突击审讯（且大多是疲劳审讯）达<span lang="EN-US">50</span>余次，身心惨遭迫害。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又因在北京南站照相，被北京市丰台公安刑拘一个月后，又被焦作市当局带回原籍补充侦查再次刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被河南省焦作市中站区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。其不服，提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日经焦作市中级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。获释后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，李玉凤在北京申诉又遭绑架押回，后被刑事拘留，直接送往焦作看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李昱函：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，现北京执业律师，<span lang="EN-US">709</span>王宇案的代理律师。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年考取律师资格，<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年开始在辽宁执业。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年为逃避公安迫害从辽宁逃到北京，目前于北京市敦信律师事务个人所执业。李昱函患有心脏疾病，并曾多次受到公安的酷刑对待。李昱函律师最后一次和外界接触是在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。当天，她向弟弟发短信，说自己被沈阳市公安局和平分局警察带走。之后便下落不明。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午，李昱函的家属对外透露，李律师现已被沈阳市公安局和平分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被正式批捕。律师已获会见。获知李昱函患有房颤心律失常、冠心病、甲亢、弥漫性胃炎等病，她包里的诊断证明都有，抓捕他在派出所里，她就感觉这次就活不成了。目前羁押在沈阳市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李玉君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东烟台龙口法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，龙口新嘉派出所丁广显、王波等多名警察，在未经允许的情况下，闯进李玉君家，看到家里有法轮功书籍和资料，打电话叫来国保大队警察郭富兑将李玉君绑架到张家沟拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6 </span>日，李玉君转刑事拘留，被送到烟台看守所非法关押。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日 ，李玉君女儿委托律师到看守所看望母亲，得知看守所里面非常热，还有蚊子咬，非常担心母亲。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，李玉君所谓的案卷送到龙口检察院。这是龙口地区敲门行动中第一起被构陷案。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日又被龙口市检察院批捕，后又将李玉君的案卷发回龙口国保大队，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日国保大队再次将构陷资料送交到龙口检察院公诉科。目前被关押在烟台看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李玉明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东德州禹城访民。因进京上访反映问题，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被禹城市警方带回当地后被控““扰乱国家机关工作秩序和敲诈勒索政府”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日家属收到逮捕通知书，目前已被超期羁押长达<span lang="EN-US">90</span>多天。据李玉明女儿李桂芝讲述，父亲李玉明因低保金被当地民政部门无故取消而上访多年，问题始终没有得到解决。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日他再次前往北京国家信访局反映述求，被山东驻京办人员截获，强制带回，直接关进了德州市看守所。李桂芝介绍，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年民政部门给父母办理了低保证明（证号为<span lang="EN-US">371484100305308</span>），两位老人一直领取政府发放的低保金。有一天，父亲去医院看病，医院告知其低保取消了，药费不报销。在没有任何告知，没有任何理由的情况下，地方民政部门擅自将父亲的低保取消了。父亲实在咽不下这口气，遂开始逐级信访反映问题。可地方政府有关部门不但不予解决他的信访问题，反而利用公权力对父亲进行截访、非法拘禁、传唤、拘留等一系列非法手段，进行打压迫害。据禹城市公安局出具的拘留通知书显示，李玉明被拘留的另一个原因是涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”。对此，李桂芝表示事实情况是：<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，父亲从济南准备乘车前往北京，在车站遭到禹城市维稳人员拦截，这些人为了达到不让他进京上访的目的，就提出救助父亲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元作为补偿，并保证在<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大期间不进京，父亲迫于无奈只好同意跟随其返回禹城，回到禹城后，对方实际先支付了<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，另<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元经多次讨要才支付。之后，父亲在<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大期间被非法限制人身自由长达<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多天。另外，因常年上访，导致家中经济窘困，父亲所住房屋无钱修复，所以他曾向当地维稳部门申请救助金，用以维修破旧的房屋，如今这也成了父亲敲诈勒索政府的证据了。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李展：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">深圳佳士案维权工人。“<span lang="EN-US">7.27</span>大抓捕”第<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初，余浚聪、米久平、刘鹏华、李展四人被正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李振环：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、山东菏泽市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十六岁，菏泽市电视台退休干部。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，程盼云、李振环、陈玉花三位法轮功女学员开着电轿车下乡，在当地农村散发法轮功真相资料，在菏泽市牡丹区安兴镇被牡丹区公安局国保大队警察跟踪抓捕。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李振洋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省朝阳市法轮功学员。李振洋是朝阳市一个普通人，是靠蹬板车或做苦力活维持生计。李振洋自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被抓捕后，一直被非法关押在朝阳市看守所。李振洋于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李志洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南周口市维权人士。李志洲因对<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年与其兄间的土地纠纷判决不满，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月项城市法院强制执行时对其殴打、辱骂，又“违法拘留”了他<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后才补齐相关手续。同时，李志洲提到回转履行不积极，造成其车辆误工三年，损失两万余元，而法院对其所称的“违法拘留”一事一直未予认定。李志洲因此长期上访。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，李志洲向周口市中院申请赔偿，李志洲在当地法院及政府工作人员的见证下，于周口市中院接收了一笔由镇政府给其的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元“困难救助”款，然而到了<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，这笔救助款突然成了他“敲诈勒索政府”的罪证。当月，李志洲被河南周口项城警方以涉嫌敲诈勒索罪刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，周口市郸城县检察院以敲诈勒索罪、寻衅滋事罪对李志洲提起公诉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，郸城县法院公开审理此案，法院合议后决定休庭，择日再审。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日第二次庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，周口市郸城县法院第三次开庭审理此案。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廉焕力：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">六四天网义工，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日前往雅安市看守所看望访民陈明燕时被警方拦截至芦山县飞仙关派出所后失联。目前遭遇强迫失踪。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">连燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东邹城法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年底连燕在向民众赠送新年台历时，遭人恶告，次日，数十个警察将连燕和丈夫绑架到派出所，几个小时后她的丈夫被放回。连燕被非法关押在枣庄市岳楼看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午，济宁市任城区法院人员在枣庄看守所对善良妇女连燕宣判，判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，鞠殿红因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">梁琴因是要犯被重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。</b>其余<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人，具体刑期不详。但此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人都因不服判决，都已提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 90.75pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁志英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省潜江市人权捍卫者帅仁兵的妻子，帅仁兵于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被潜江市公安局以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后关押在潜江市看守所并被批准逮捕。帅仁兵目前已被超期羁押长达两年半的时间，此案至今没有开庭，其妻梁志英因为夫鸣冤，也遭抓捕刑拘。据悉，帅仁兵是湖北省潜江市人，因遭遇暴力强拆而上访，曾因上访被多次围追、堵截、绑架、非法拘禁、拘留、暴力毒打迫害。<span lang="EN-US"> 2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日因进京上访维权被抓走失联，他的妻儿于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日在潜江市人民政府门前举牌寻人未果。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日其家人收到潜江市公安局出具的被刑拘人员通知书，才得知帅仁兵被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，关押在潜江市看守所，之后被批准逮捕。目前帅仁兵已被超期羁押长达两年半的时间，此案至今没有开庭。其妻梁志英因多次进京为夫鸣冤，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被潜江市园林镇书记雇人，将母子两人强行从北京绑架回潜江当地，后被非法拘禁在黑监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底梁志英亦被刑事拘留，目前关押在潜江市看守所。梁志英从去年底被关进潜江拘留所以后，就再也没有任何消息发出。访民们只知道他们夫妻两个育有两个孩子，大的已经成年，小的大概只有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>岁的样子，目前梁志英被关在拘留所里，小儿子不知被谁在照顾。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁子亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东鹤山市沙坪街道浸信教会传道人，梁子亮与妻子李银秀，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日带领信徒在当地一公园内拉横幅反对堕胎以及传福音，当晚被警察传唤到派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，梁子亮与妻子李银秀的家属，接到鹤山市公安局发出的刑事拘留通知书，两份通知书分别指梁子梁和李银秀，违反刑事诉讼法第八十条之规定，涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集罪，刑事拘留，现羁押在鹤山市看守所。据信徒介绍，梁子亮原是当地官办三自教会的信徒，后离开“三自”，成立家庭教会。目前，浸信教会有信徒约二十人。每周举行聚会，梁子亮还会带领信徒外出传福音，也因此多次受到警察警告。广东省基督教因传福音被刑事拘留的案子，并不多见。很多教会担心当局此举是为了震慑其他家庭教会，以阻止信徒外出传福音。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廖杰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、大连市庄河市法轮功学员。廖杰于<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日出生，家居庄河市长岭镇。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午，她在蓉花山镇双烈寺集讲真相被蓉花山镇派出所警察抓捕。当日下午，警察上门抄家，抢劫了一些私人物品。廖杰被关押在姚家看守所，后被构陷到庄河市法院，遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廖松林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">生于<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，湖南郴州市军人接待站退休职工，法轮功学员。廖松林<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被绑架到洗脑班关押；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被抓捕，关押在郴州市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被郴州市北湖区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押在湖南常德津市监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年又被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，合计已<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年冤刑。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，郴州市北湖区国保大队，在没有出示任何合法手续、证件的情况下，绑架了七十七岁的法轮功学员廖松林。之后，五个警察强行进入廖松林家抄家，将法轮功书籍、九千多元人民币等私人物品全部抄走。随后，廖松林被关押在郴州市看守所。期间，七十七岁高龄的廖松林被医生检测出身患高血压、冠心病、轻微脑梗、肺结核等病症。因此缘故，廖松林被转到一九八医院继续关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，湖南省郴州市北湖区法院判处廖松林<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林后勤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福清维权公民，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月初，林后勤等十多位维权人士前往北京上访被截回并立即全部被刑拘，目前十多位维权人士都已取保侯审，仅林后勤遭批捕起诉。起诉书中指控：林后勤曾出现在福州省高院，福建维权公民每周三“每周一聚”的抗议维权中。林后勤进京上访被寻衅滋事案，由人权律师山东张金武律师代理，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>号上午张金武律师冒雨前往福清看守所会见林后勤。 目前林后勤精神状态良好，坚持认定自己上访无罪，谢绝律师为其办理取保侯审的建议，要求当局无罪释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林景萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。林景萍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林丽芳</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁，福建省柘荣县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，因与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、庄友布、陈开奇、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中林丽芳被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林丽珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东茂名市电白区水东镇法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>林燕梅与姐姐林丽珍、外甥吴朝琪（林丽珍的儿子）一家三人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被茂名市滨海新区公安分局抓捕。林燕梅、林丽珍、吴朝棋在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被电白区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林明华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：辽宁省沈阳市著名维权人士林明洁的哥哥。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与弟弟林明洁一起遭抓捕，据悉已被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林明洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">是辽宁省沈阳市铁西区人，原辽宁省某国企技术人员，人称“访民义侠”，维权公民，人权捍卫者，曾获得海外中国民主党颁发的曹顺利勇气奖。早年因不服其兄林明华被行政拘留和家里拆迁补偿的问题而走上信访之路，后因长期到京上访，并热心为访民维权发声而屡遭当局非法绑架、关押、拘留等打击迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁因在北京国家信访局、住建部反映地方政府违法强拆事宜，被沈阳市驻京办等截访人员跟踪骚扰，后被强行遣返原籍，并被沈阳市铁西区警方予以刑事拘留，一个月后才得以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又因和一批沈阳访民在中国公安部六部口信访局集体上访（简称“集访”），状告沈阳市公安局与局长许文有徇私枉法，随后被沈阳市截访人员抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被沈阳市铁西区警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，并控诉其罪状：在北京多次集访扰乱公共秩序、在庆安徐纯合案时打出“我是访民，朝我开枪”的标语、长期将访民维权的新闻发给境外媒体等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日止。此前曾被羁押于沈阳市铁西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，林明洁结束两年多的监狱生活刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与哥哥林明华一起遭警方抓捕，据悉已被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林生亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林生亮是深圳市某企业财务人员，维权公民。近年来，因积极活跃于网络线上线下各种社会维权活动，尤其是在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年深圳<span lang="EN-US">11.15</span>大抓捕后，他积极为被捕的维权同道呼吁，积极专注于江西赣州明经国抗强拆杀村官事件和四川泸州市泸县太伏中学学生赵鑫坠亡事件等等，而被当局公安国保秘密监控。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底，由于为了传播涉及中共高层贪腐的“郭文贵爆料”讯息，在摩拜单车上涂写“上推特、关注郭文贵”等字句，并在网上转发，而被深圳警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后被转正式逮捕，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被深圳市宝安区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底刑满释放。林生亮又于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被警方拘捕，现关押宝安看守所。后获知，林生亮被中共当局以寻衅滋事判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林燕梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东茂名市电白区水东镇法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>林燕梅与姐姐林丽珍、外甥吴朝琪（林丽珍的儿子）一家三人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被茂名市滨海新区公安分局抓捕。林燕梅、林丽珍、吴朝棋在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被电白区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林应强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福州“<span lang="EN-US">9.12</span>”事件当事人之一。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日出生，福建省福州市人，福州市仓山区失地农民，实名举报者，维权代表，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年期间，曾因所在区域土地被强征，地方当局非法截留征地款达近千万元，致使众多村民陷入生存困境，随作为村民代表就此多次向有关部门予以举报、控告维权，但却遭到地方当局管理者的严厉打击和报复；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾被时任仓山区委书记的张森兴（现已因贪污而被捕入狱）以约谈为由骗至管理部门大楼，被多名打手打伤，其紧急报警，当地警方却对此“不作为”；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾在护送儿子去幼儿园的途中被三名手持铁棍的歹徒暴打，其再次报警，当地警方竟再度对此“不作为”；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其被福州市仓山区警方突然以涉嫌“邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被福州市仓山区法院经二审以“敲诈勒索罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并在福清监狱服刑；出狱后，其坚称自己无罪；由于其不畏艰险，坚持多次为失地农民维权和举报贪官张文灿，故而多次遭遇不幸；曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被当局指派的黑社会人员追杀致伤，曾被构陷枉判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，曾被警方多次非法行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，曾因到北京上访时在美国大使馆门前告洋状，而被北京警方训诫并责令返遣返回乡，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天后又被福州市警方以涉嫌“妨害执行公务罪”拘留<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，因再次到北京上访而被福州市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后被当地检察院正式批捕，并被关押在福州市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被福建省福州市长乐县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，刑满出狱；据悉，其狱中曾遭酷刑虐待，受探视权被长期剥夺。此前在福建省仓山监狱（福州市仓山区螺洲镇敖山工业区，仓山监狱二监区五分监区，邮编<span lang="EN-US">350019</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，福州公民与严兴声太太及亲属共<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多人去迎接严兴声先生出狱，因在福州第一看守所门口放鞭炮，被警方带走。后被刑事拘留、逮捕、起诉。目前在押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，福州市仓山区法院就<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日福州维权人士放鞭炮迎良心犯的福州“鞭炮案”，一审宣判。福州著名维权人士林应强和唐兆星均被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，林兰英判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。林应强刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林永旭：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">珠海市香洲区法轮功学员、原飞机制造设计工程。因为坚持法轮功信仰，曾被关洗脑班和劳教，累计迫害逾七年。林永旭于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在家被珠海市公安局拱北口岸分局绑架、关押，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被判三年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款三千元。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日又被劫持到广东省北江监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林在务：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，化名林大海、林忠，福建省福清市人，福清市东瀚镇东瀚村田尾<span lang="EN-US">17</span>号村民，职业不详，“耶和华见证人”信徒、传道人，新疆耶和华见证人教会正规先驱（类似于基督教的长老），中国在押良心犯。因信仰耶和华见证人教派，并被委任在新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒地区做正规先驱（即该教会一种重要职务），在库尔勒市组成家庭聚会，举行上百次大型聚会及成员培训，大力发展信徒，随遭极左思维极强的中共当局严打狠批；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，在“耶和华见证人案”大抓捕中，被库尔勒市警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”与多人悉数抓捕、刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式逮捕，并被指控称，其因打着基督教旗号，组织教会聚会， “宣扬所谓政治中立，煽动成员及他人不履行公民法定义务”，破坏了国家的法律法规，所以属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人涉邪教案被警方向当地检察院提起公诉；后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被检察院发回补帧，但同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又已被补查重报；至今待审未判，且无更多具体信息；据悉，曾在看守所内因拒绝唱“红歌”等，常遭连体铐、抱铐等体罚虐待。目前被羁押于库尔勒市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">凌浩波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;
