lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生于湖北省随州市，近年在广州工作生活。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日凌浩波在广东华登（河源市）玩具制品有限公司被警方带走，原因和去向不明。此前，凌浩波因为关注邓传彬被刑事拘留一案并在推特发布邓案的相关消息，于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被广州白云区公安分局传唤，随后凌浩波回到老家湖北随州。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日凌浩波返回广州后被白云区嘉禾房东告知：已应警察要求注销其门卡，强迫其搬迁；凌浩波<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日到河源工厂上班，<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被警方带走后失联。目前已确认于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被刑事拘留，关押在河源市看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘爱香：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘长富并抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对刘长富、李国爱、吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。刘长富刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘春兰（辽宁）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省抚顺市望花区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，刘春兰、刘邵君被望花公安分局建设派出所警察非法抓走。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被辽宁省抚顺市望花区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘德明：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，南通市公安局港闸分局以涉嫌故意毁坏财产罪为由，将南通市港闸区永兴街道节制闸村村民刘德明带走调查。次日，该局作出港公（公）拘通字【<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>】<span lang="EN-US">263</span>号拘留通知书，载明对刘德明刑事拘留，现羁押于南通市看守所，并将拘留通知书向刘德明妻子送达。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日一早，无执法权的南通欣宏房屋征收服务有限公司受南通市港闸区住房和建设环境保护局委托，雇佣一批保安拥着挖掘机（犯罪工具），进入南通市港闸区永兴街道节制闸村，将刘德明的房屋团团围住，并拉上了警戒线，企图强拆，以达到非法圈地的目的。村民们向<span lang="EN-US">110</span>报警。港闸公安分局民警到达现场后，只是谈谈地说了一句：“政府行为，我们管不了”，致使非法圈地的保安更加有恃无恐，对刘德明家围困了整整一夜。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，该公司雇佣的保安用铁锤敲打刘德明的房屋。情势危急，且在民警不作为的情况下，刘德明为捍卫家园才点燃钩机。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘飞跃：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">民生观察工作室负责人。湖北随州市人，自其<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年创办民生观察工作室以来，每逢敏感时期都会遭到来自随州当局以非法维稳为目的非法拘禁，和极不人道的殴打等形式的迫害、威胁，甚至殃及家属。刘飞跃先生<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日已被随州市公安局带走并刑事拘留，据消息称其罪名为涉嫌颠覆国家政权，起初其家属未得到书面通知。目前律师已经会见。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日刘飞跃先生涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案，在湖北随州市中院宣判，刘飞跃获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘贵荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省大同市灵丘县法轮功学员。刘贵荣依法信访，反映法轮功学员被基层公检法人员抓捕、滥用职权枉法追诉，而遭打击报复，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日早上五点多，刘贵荣等又一次被灵丘县国保警察从家里抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被大同市云岗区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，家属提起上诉，二审在没有履行任何程序的情况下维持原判，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日刘贵荣被送山西省女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘国霞</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河北省承德县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被河北省承德县警方抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被河北省承德县法院一审以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘家玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津静海县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年四十六岁。原静海县市容环卫局干部，静海县静海镇高庄子村人。她曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年两次被非法关押在天津大港区板桥女子劳教所，前后五年遭受强制奴役劳动、不让睡觉等迫害，她坚持信仰，不妥协。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年才出狱。刘家玲<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，被关押在天津女子监狱，遭受残忍迫害。刘家玲在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日又失踪，后得知被关押在静海看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获知刘家玲又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，在天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘建霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省三门峡人，五十多岁，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年七二零后，因去北京为法轮大法鸣冤而遭抓捕，后被非法劳教，劫持到郑州十八里河劳教所，后来又被三门峡法院判刑六年。她曾被迫流离失所多年。三门峡“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>” 到处查找她，在全国非法通缉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刘建霞与法轮功学员杨中省被跟踪抓捕。刘建霞曾在河南省新乡女子监狱被关小号折磨<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多天，被迫害得脸肿、胸闷等“哮喘”症状已经一年多，现在越来越重，生命垂危，据悉每天靠大量药物维持生存。当年与刘建霞一起被抓捕的法轮功学员杨中省，被非法关押没有几天，就于二零一六年四月在郑州第三看守所被迫害致死。刘建霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘建新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建访民。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，福建省福州市仓山区城门镇前锦村的江国英，突然接到城门镇赵书记的电话，说其丈夫刘建新已经从北京接回来了，公安局要对其刑事拘留。江国英说：我丈夫刘建新因房屋被拆除近<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年了，至今无补偿、无安置，在家又要被<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时监控，感到非常郁闷，去北京旅游散心，刘建新在北京没有信访，更没有违法行为，怎么会被刑拘？随后仓山区公安分局城门派出所通知江国英，说刘建新已经被送到福州市第二看守所关押。目前尚不知被构陷的罪名，估计是针对维权访民的口袋罪——寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东枣庄市薛城区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘杰和魏延景出去张贴法轮功宣传不干胶被永福派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，山东枣庄市薛城区法院开庭宣判，判决刘杰<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金三万元，魏延景<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并罚金五千元。刘杰当庭宣布上诉。刘杰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘金英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京大兴采育镇<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁的法轮功学员刘金英、一直被关押在大兴看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁沈阳的维权人士。刘丽是为父亲刘树义劳工权益而上访了十一年。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，时年已经<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁的刘树义为了活命，还在沈阳市苏家屯八一镇政府内烧锅炉，为里面“全心全意为人民服务”的官员做苦力。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">19</span>点，加班的刘树义在上班途中遭遇车祸，按照劳动合同法的规定，用人单位应该以工伤予以补偿，但八一镇政府因为没有为劳动者办理工伤保险，就拒绝承担工伤责任，作为女儿的刘丽开始替父上访维权。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘丽到了北京府右街后被截访送马家楼，然而有沈阳市苏家屯区的截访人员接回。后遭刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘敏杰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河北省保定市定州市人，人称“维权能手”，人权捍卫者。曾因儿子刘强从部队退伍后做生意被抢劫杀害，而最高法院未公开审理就直接改判，以致主凶未受到应有的惩罚，随认为此举属于认定事实错误、违反法定程序，从而进京上访维权十余年，其间，其申诉冤案不仅没得到纠正，反被属地和北京等司法机关以莫须有的罪名劳教、拘留多次，还被接访官员打断几根肋骨，且因多次被毒打，患上神经性脊髓炎，眼睛也几近失明。近年来，因其在北京最高检、最高法、国家信访局，全国人大信访接待处及中央领导、巡视组寄信继续揭露最高法院的办案黑幕，虽引起中纪委等领导重视，但却遭到最高法院等司法部门的打击报复，曾被最高法院法警多次殴打、关小黑屋虐待，被地方公检法以各种方式截访等。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日其被最高法院法警和北京东交民巷派出所警方突然联合抓捕，次日被移交至河北省定州市警方，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-23</span>日先后被以涉“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘和逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被河北省定州市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服，已当庭提起上诉。目前被关押在河北省定州市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘鹏华： </span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">佳士案维权工人。“<span lang="EN-US">7.27</span>大抓捕”第<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初，刘鹏华、余浚聪、米久平、李展等四人被正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘芊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，山东泰安肥城市法轮功学员、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十三岁，原肥城市实验小学教师。因坚持修炼法轮功被非法劳教一年、冤判五年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被肥城市公安局非法拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被批捕。刘芊被关押在泰安市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，山东泰安肥城市法院判刘芊<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款三万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="background: white; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘庆杰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="background: white; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林长春法轮功学员。法轮功学员王淑华的丈夫李国军到长春市找工作，还不到十天，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚二十时许，长春市民康路派出所警察六、七人，突然闯入南关区西四道街宏达小区三栋五单元<span lang="EN-US">709</span>室法轮功学员刘庆杰的租房，将刚刚进屋的刘庆杰、李国军抓捕。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">长春市南关区法院<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日判决法轮功学员<span style="background: white;">刘庆杰<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘庆强</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：广东省惠东县人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，刘庆强与周育琴、石雪梅<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被惠东县政法委、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办及国保等警方非法抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密宣判。其中，刘庆强被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；周育琴被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金五万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；石雪梅被冤判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；三人均不服审判，已向广东省惠州市中级法院提出上诉。目前被关押在惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘仁秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连市旅顺法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">48</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前被关押在大连市监狱第五监区。据悉，监狱非法剥夺了他家人的探视权。家人已经有约半年多的时间没有见到他了。刘仁秋是在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被特警在其租住房内抓捕。当天，大连政法委策划，采用手机监控、跟踪、定位、蹲坑等手段，在大连地区各县区同一时间统一行动，抓捕了数十名法轮功学员，有很多人当天被放回，有的当月回家，最后还有多人被判刑。这次抓捕被公安国保称为“<span lang="EN-US">1614</span>”大案。刘仁秋、盛杰、谷树春、王红玉四名法轮功学员，被旅顺法院二次非法开完庭后，在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下判决书， 刘仁秋被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚款五万元；盛杰<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半、罚款三万元；王红玉<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半、罚金款三千。刘仁秋刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘邵君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省抚顺市望花区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，刘春兰、刘邵君被望花公安分局建设派出所警察非法抓走。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被辽宁省抚顺市望花区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘嗣堂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省济南市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十六岁。退休前原是济南市钢铁总公司设备制造公司机动科科长兼技术工程师。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，刘嗣堂夫妻在济南天桥区桑梓店集市赶集向民众讲法轮功真相、发放法轮功真相资料，被天桥区公安分局桑梓店派出所警察抓捕，后因年龄大当天被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，济南市天桥区检察院以刘嗣堂有所谓的“前科”（曾被非法判刑五年半）对他进行批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，刘嗣堂被济南市天桥区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘淑芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西大同法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，大同市刘淑芳因给当权者寄信反映法轮功学员被迫害的事实，遭到公检法部门的打击报复，一周后被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。这已是刘淑芳第三次被迫害。第一次是因依法起诉江泽民迫害法轮功，遭到打击报复，行政拘留十五日。第二次是因依信访条例给当权者寄信，反映法轮功学员被基层公检法人员绑架、滥用职权枉法追诉，而被打击报复，行政拘留十五日，这次依然是因给当权者寄信，在家门口被监控绑架。这一次直接判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘卫国：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，北京市丰台区人，化名刘于谦，北京源佳科技公司职员，自由信仰者，新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒市常驻居民，“耶和华见证人”教派信徒，前重庆会众长老，前新疆伊犁会众长老，库尔勒会众长老，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，自从在北京基督某教派“耶和华见证人”受洗以来，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年被派往重庆举行传教，后被安立（任命）为重庆会众长老；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又前往新疆伊犁市做伊犁会众长老；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又被任命库尔勒会众长老；因曾大力发展教会信徒，举办会众参加圣经培训及举办<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多次家庭聚会，从而引起库尔勒市当局关注；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因曾两次参加“耶和华见证人”香港分部的区域大会，后又在库尔勒楼兰世家组织聚会，随被库尔勒市民宗委查处；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，因曾到韩国参加过区域大会，遂再遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，与多人被巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒市警方悉数抓捕刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪 ”转正式被捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人被库尔勒市检察院提起公诉，指控其所属教会与正统基督教教义不符，宣传“政治中性”，要求信徒“不履行国家宪法，不参加爱国主义教育，不服兵役，不入党，不如团，不升国旗，不唱国歌，不向国旗敬礼”等，同时又打着基督教旗号，积极发展组织成员，多次组织、提供场所进行聚会，故而触犯了政府法律规定，属于参与邪教的违法行为；截至目前，其具体信息缺详，至今未审待判。目前被羁押于库尔勒市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘文廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省沧州市盐山县法轮功学员。）杨月亮、刘文廷在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日给人安装卫星电视接收器（据称可收看新唐人电视台）时遭圣佛镇派出所警察抓捕，后被非法关押在盐山县看守所。杨月亮被非法关押近一个月后遭盐山县检察院非法批捕。刘文廷被非法刑拘一个月时遭勒索保证金后“取保”回家。取保半年后，又被“监视居住”近一年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，刘文廷再次遭关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，杨月亮遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；刘文廷被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘湘菊</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：辽宁省沈阳市辽中区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刘湘菊在向村民发放法轮功真相台历时，被辽中区公安局警察绑架。第二天，辽中区城郊派出所警察去她家抄家，在她家无人的情况下，私自掠走了她丈夫打工挣来的九千元现金。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，刘湘菊女士被辽中区法院非法庭审，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下达判决书，被非法判刑七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘秀莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省七旬法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日早上九点，刘秀莲在绥化北林区水利五处被等在这里的绥化北林区“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”成员绑架到公安局。据称，起因是，在两个月内，市政府附近街道两边出现了三十多个“法轮大法好”、“真善忍好”条幅。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，黑龙江海伦法院以 “利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪” 判刑刘秀莲<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至 <span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;
