12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省烟台市牟平区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十五岁。刘学荣老人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午在牟平区集贸市场发法轮大法资料，被便衣警察绑架，随后被关押到烟台市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，牟平区公检法机构秘密对老人判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被关押到济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘艳丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生于<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年，湖北荆门公民，人权捍卫者。原是荆门市一间银行的职员。刘艳丽是因网上公布与国保的对话记录，因言获罪<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日遭刑事拘留，罪名竟然是“诽谤罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日又被逮捕。共被羁押了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>）取保获释。刘艳丽主要做帮助抗战老兵工作，是一名追求民主自由人士，网上言论较多，是一位政治异见人士。刘艳丽<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午开始被荆门公安国保传唤。后获知刘艳丽遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刘艳丽女士因言获罪，被荆门市东宝区法院以寻衅滋事罪判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省抚顺市清原县<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁的法轮功学员，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> </b><span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在贴“法轮大法好”粘贴时被警察绑架，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日遭清原县法院庭审，后被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年的一天，经人介绍刘玉开始学炼法轮功。刘玉曾患有胃癌，因修炼法轮功才得以康复。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功后，刘玉用自己的亲身经历向民众讲述大法的美好，揭穿中共喉舌媒体谎言。为此刘玉多次遭绑架、关押：<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年冬天被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日再次被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被绑架，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；回家不到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘玉于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日再次被绑架，后又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘玉霞</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，现年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁，河南省平顶山市人，原在市政府物价局工作，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功遭迫害，曾被多次送“洗脑班”、拘留，甚至被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并在新乡女子监狱服刑，遭非人虐待，同时被单位开除，无任何生活来源。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午七点多，刘玉霞在路上发邀请函，请人们旁听法轮功信仰者穆亚东的庭审，结果又被光明路派出所抓捕，后关押到平顶山宝丰县看守所。由于刘玉霞不报姓名，直到下午七点，派出所根据手纹用技术手段才查出刘玉霞的身份和住址。晚上八点，其家被查抄，搜走法轮功书籍多本、未发出去的邀请函及几个真相光盘等。随后，她就被刑拘和逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刘玉霞被平顶山市新华区法院一审重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千。其不服上诉，后经平顶山市中级法院不公开审理，依然维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日她已被送往到河南省新乡女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘永泽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">公益机构长沙富能工作人员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌颠覆国家政权罪刑拘，现羁押在湖南省国家安全厅看守所。长沙富能一直通过政府信息公开的方式尝试促进政府透明度、通过规范性文件审查的方式督促各级政府部门的红头文件合法性、通过建议信和立法倡导方式促进残疾人和乙肝、艾滋携带者等群体的平等权利。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘中花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省莱西市法轮功学员。刘中花被莱西市法院非法判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被送往山东省女子监狱。刘中花曾于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。此次被非法判刑，是因为她给警察讲真相而被劫持构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刘中花到日庄镇派出所给警察讲述法轮大法，警察将刘中花扣押并送入大牢。次刘中花被抓，她家人的一切权利全被剥夺，其家人直到收到山东省女子监狱的信才知道刘中花被判刑并被送进监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳德玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省荆门市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，曾多次遭到迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月历经<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年残酷迫害后，从范家台监狱黑窝回家。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在讲法轮功时又被绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，荆门市东宝区法院庭审柳德玉，历时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分钟。当场未宣布刑期。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获知，柳德玉被冤判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被转到湖北沙洋范家台监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">龙克海<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原籍甘肃徽县的龙克海长期居住在陕西宝鸡，多年来因批评政府成为被当地警方严控的对象，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月曾因在社交媒体上嘲讽毛泽东、习近平等人被抓捕。目前龙克海的微号帐号已被封锁，龙克海于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在陕西省宝鸡市与外界失联，虽经多方寻找甚至是向警方报案仍未有其下落，直到近日龙克海的儿子龙少腾了解到，龙克海于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被宝鸡市渭滨区警察带走后在指定居所监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">38</span>天后又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。原因可能是持续在网络发言，批评和讽刺政府和国家主席习近平。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底，龙克海因被控寻衅滋事案获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卢凤花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十五岁，家住青岛市西海岸新区胶南办事处象沟头村。在中共迫害法轮功持续至今近二十年中，卢凤花曾被判刑八年，在济南监狱被迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在家包粽子，被胶南派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被胶南检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被黄岛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卢丽斯、卢丽贞、卢思灵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州市花都区花山镇村民，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，卢家土地被花山镇政府因肇花高速公路建设征地而被强拆强征。自强拆后当月，卢家举家赴京上访多次，累遭各种打击报复：绑架、恐吓、毒打、黑监狱禁锢和刑事迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，卢丽贞（刚产子不满一年，尚在法定保护的哺乳期妇女）、卢思灵、卢丽斯三人被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪和破坏生产经营罪”刑拘；女儿卢丽铧遭多次非法行政拘留，诉讼到区、市、省三级法院都遭不公判决。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，三人被广州市花都区分局以涉嫌“破坏生产经营罪”而逮捕，现羁押于花都区看守所。现情况不明。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陆惠平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陆惠平、陆宗并、黄志球一家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人是福建屏南奇案——一家四口<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被刑事拘留、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人被强迫失踪的当事人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日陆惠平的妹妹陆晶发了一条“父母和姐姐无罪”的微博后，屏南县城关派出所公安上门抓人至今未归。本案简介：陆惠平<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，到屏南县古峰镇长汾社区复印承包地确权材料，全程录音显示陆惠平与工作人员双方都很平和，长汾社区副区长挑起事端，突然窜出殴打陆惠平，声称确权材料是国家秘密，不给复印并招来屏南城关派出所公安，拘留了陆惠平。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日拘留十天期满，陆母黄志球到拘留所接陆惠平回家时双双当场被抓捕，同日陆父陆宗并在家被抓捕。一家三口被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。然而，屏南当局对陆家征地分文未补，陆父在征地现场被打断肋骨，陆母气绝服农药险酿命案，该案至今未处理。普通百姓敲诈强大的政府，这逻辑相当怪异。此案于是<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，罪名摇身一变“破坏生产经营罪”，并于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日执行逮捕，陆惠平和母亲黄志球羁押在宁德看守所，陆父陆宗并羁押在屏南看守所。全家三口被刑拘后，屏南古峰镇政府被福州中院认定“强占土地违法”的情况下，再次开工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日， “福建屏南奇案”陆惠平一家三口被“破坏生产经营罪”一审在屏南法院第二法庭公开宣判，黄志求被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。陆惠平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陆建华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，上海市人，前中国最高层核心智囊之一，第二届“北京市十大杰出青年”，曾任中国社会科学院社会学研究所研究员、公共政策研究中心副主任，中央电视台特约评论员和重庆市渝北区副区长等职，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，因陆续为香港记者程翔提供<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余篇稿件，其中<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月所提供的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>篇文章内容被中共视为涉及“国家绝密资料”，遂于<span lang="EN-US"> 2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被国家安全局秘密拘捕；后经秘密审判，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市第二中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US"> 20</span>年；其上诉坚称自己被冤，均被驳回。目前在北京市监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陆建荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏讨薪农民工、维权公民。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年先后两次于六四敏感日因转发中国公民及国际友人在驻美中国大使馆门口举行纪念“六<span lang="EN-US">.</span>四”活动的图片遭到警方传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日又被江苏警方跨省抓捕，涉嫌“非法买卖枪支弹药罪”，至今不被释放，被刑拘于泰兴市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陆祚钰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建失地农民、维权人士。陆祚钰是福建省屏南县古汾镇长汾村人，一家<span lang="EN-US">8</span>口人共十余亩耕地，靠种植蘑菇和养猪的收入维持生活。到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，全家的耕地被政府动用暴力强行征用，一家人还多人被政府雇佣的征地人员打伤，报警公安不予理睬，陆祚钰为此走访各级政府，反映地方政府违法征用耕地的行为，结果是屡屡遭到打击报复，甚至被判刑入狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底因北京上访被拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被行政拘留九天期满，于当日上午八点被公安以“寻衅滋事”立即传唤，并于当天下午三点以口袋罪“寻衅滋事”升级为刑拘，羁押于宁德看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鲁•贡确嘉措：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青海省黄南州尖扎县拉莫德钦寺僧人，因写书记录流亡印度觐见达赖喇嘛尊者的经历，近日第二次遭当局带走，目前与外界失联。鲁•贡确嘉措将自己翻越雪山、赴印拜见达赖喇嘛尊者的过程，写成名为《五十四天》的书籍，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年年底完稿后被警方约谈，带到黄南州国安局非法扣留审问长达一周之久，并被警告不得出版该书。获释后不满一个月，贡确嘉措再次被当局约谈，目前与外界失联。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，黄南州统战部打电话约谈，他回复说等雪停了后再去，结果下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分左右，两名黄南州安全局的人员将他带走，之后便没有了任何消息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鲁扬</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：现年<span lang="EN-US">49</span>岁，本名张桂祺，网名“鲁西狂徒”，山东省莘县人，著名诗人。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年开始诗歌文学创作活动，创办“扬子宛诗社”，并主编出版《扬子宛诗刊》。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年创办“中国当代诗歌论坛”，出版主编《中国当代诗歌》刊物。二年后“中国当代诗论坛”被封。期间开始在《星星》、《诗选刊》等国内著名诗歌刊物上发表诗歌。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年创办“中国自由文化论坛”，因颇有影响而被迫多次关停，后移入外网“自由中国”网站，最后又移入博讯网站。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因自由写作被迫于聊城外国学校辞职，后妻子工作也受到牵连，一起离开山东，南方谋生，此间由诗歌创作转入文化自由写作，大量作品发表于国内各大网站，并被海外多家网站转载。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年参与“零八宪章”签署，夫妻工作再次受到影响，双双失业。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，为支持入狱的本会前会长刘晓波而入独立中文笔会。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年受“茉莉花运动”影响，再次失业并遭遣返回山东老家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因举牌声援批评毛泽东遭解职的山东广播电视台特约评论员邓相超教授，在邓教授所在的济南建筑大学遭到暴徒殴打，受到中外媒体关注，同时也成为有关部门重点监控对象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年创办“中国诗人大讲堂——文殊书院”，继续从事自由文化传播事业。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方带走，下落不明近两个星期，后被聊城市公安局以“涉嫌颠覆国家政权罪”宣布刑事拘留，后遭正式逮捕，关押于聊城市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">栾凝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">，男，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十岁，大学文化，原来在宁夏劳动人事厅工作，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功前，是宁夏法轮功辅导站副站长（义务教功）。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，栾凝到兴庆区一邮政储蓄所邮寄信件。栾凝离开后，被该所人员以信件涉及法轮功内容向派出所报警，并将信件交给派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，栾凝上班时在家门口被抓捕。宁夏银川市中级法院在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下达判决书，对栾凝判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛迪嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区索县若达乡索卡村人，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">Lodoe Gyamtso</span>，西藏民间舞蹈艺术家，藏族人权捍卫者，异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代初，曾因其姐、妹二人在一场车祸中被司机撞死及遭到谋杀，而当时的那曲地方法院竟枉法以该司机为亲共藏人为由，判其“无罪”；同年晚些时候，两人在村庄市场相遇，随发生争执冲突，冲突中为了躲避司机方对其的两次射杀，其被迫自卫，刺伤了司机，致使该司机虽送医院仍最终死亡；针此，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被西藏那曲中级法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后送拉萨市扎奇监狱服刑；服刑期间，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又曾因在扎奇监狱带领狱友高喊“西藏独立”，“中国退出西藏”，“祈愿达赖喇嘛尊者长久住世”，“六百万藏人要团结”等口号进行抗议，并散发手写传单<span lang="EN-US">300</span>多份，在遭受审讯及酷刑折磨<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月之后，被西藏当局决定处于死刑，后在联合国及国际特赦等组织的干预下，才未对其施行处决，但又加刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并被转至拉萨市曲水监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其终获刑满获释，但又被软禁在家<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因公开谴责中共西藏当局强迫居住在西藏巴青县、索县和比如县的藏人中共八一建军节时穿珍贵野兽皮毛饰品（此为传统藏人服饰，但藏人已从<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年始自愿放弃穿戴该饰品）和表演歌舞等，并将其认同的达赖喇嘛提出的解决西藏问题的“中间道路”和“和平区”等概念，以及对佛教姻缘和非暴力原则重要性的感悟和认识，让其妻噶吉拍录视频，广为传播，而遭致当局的仇视与严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，又曾因公开反对中共当局强令除在西藏之外，在藏区其他各地寺院里学习的僧侣、尼师必须限期返回索县和比如县等，否则其家属将面临遭监禁和接受禁止挖虫草处罚等非人道作法（挖虫草是当地藏人经济收入的最主要来源），随再遭当局拘押，并关押在比如县监狱中，后因健康状况不佳，才准予释放；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因在拉萨市布达拉宫前举行抗议活动，并在网上发视频，宣称自己正在发起一场“世界和平运动”，引起海外流亡藏人广泛热议，随被那曲地区索县警方再次拘捕，并被以“国家机密案”论处；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其被西藏自治区那曲县中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”再次重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2036</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。目前在拉萨市扎什监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛米（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，本名嘉央，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县麦尔玛乡三村人，阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，格尔登寺闻思辩经学院般若班学员，非暴力追求者，藏族知名作家，中国在押良心犯。因长期在藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺闻思辩经学院般若班学习，且爱撰写发表、出版许多相关文章及书籍（如《弥漫的橙黄烟雾》等），从而成为海内外藏人区域知名的僧人作家，又因平素崇尚非暴力，致力于藏母语保护宣传，深受藏人及境内外网友喜爱；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被阿坝县警方突然秘密抓捕，罪由不清，自此失联；其家人、亲友及寺庙僧侣等均感震惊、担忧，其同为作家的友人疑称可能与其发表、撰写了关乎西藏命运的文章，尤其从事了环保活动有关；后知其被当局转正式逮捕，并关押于汶川县看守所；羁押期间，其饱受酷刑折磨，并在庭审前曾被利诱，要求为官方做事，称其若答应则可为其家人提供经济援助，并准其出境旅游等，若不答应则将重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，但被其断然拒绝；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其案被阿坝藏族羌族自治州法院秘密庭审，最终在未通知家属旁听的情况下被以“颠覆国家政权罪”、“泄漏国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。目前在四川省汶川监狱（德阳市黄许镇阿坝监狱或绵阳市川北监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑慈诚（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，藏族良心犯。洛桑慈诚和洛桑祥曲两名年轻僧人于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底被当地警方从格尔登寺院抓走后，长达<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个多月一直没有任何消息。他们被当局指控涉嫌与自焚僧人扎白事件有关。洛桑慈诚，是阿坝县求吉玛乡人，当年<span lang="EN-US">19</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月上旬被当局秘密（没有通知家属情况下）判处<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑次仁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县格德寺僧人，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在阿坝县城街道上，手持一幅达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，呼喊着“嘉瓦丹增嘉措万岁”疾步行走，独自游街表达了对达赖喇嘛尊者的虔诚信仰，随后被中共公安人员控制带走。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑丹增（藏<span lang="EN-US">/</span>左贡寺高僧）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年左右出生，西藏自治区昌都市左贡县旺达镇乌雅村人，又称乌雅•朱古（即转世喇嘛）洛桑丹增仁波切，早年曾在阿里地区任职导游和司机，后成为西藏左贡寺高僧。曾因经常到西藏的左贡县左贡寺劝导僧俗民众停止供奉所谓的“朵杰凶天”，而要为西藏民族的长远理想和第十四世达赖喇嘛的健康长寿着想，并鼓励藏人努力保护、发扬民族宗教与文化等，受到藏人僧俗的广泛爱戴和尊敬，随招致中共当局的恐慌和严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在西藏拉萨市被左贡县警方抓走刑拘，后被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初，被西藏自治区左贡县法院以“追随达赖分裂集团”、“劝诫、蛊惑地方藏民停止修供凶天”等为罪由，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑多吉（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1983</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州阿坝县贾柯河牧场人，阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。自幼在甘孜藏族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺出家为僧，曾因屡次谈论有关涉藏敏感话题而遭四川当局的严控打压；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾因政治诉求而遭阿坝县警方抓捕，后被阿坝县法院以不知名罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；近年来，因中共当局加大了对所有藏区僧俗的严管力度，尤其是在阿坝县注入大量维稳经费对所辖网络、电话等通讯管道予以严控，并对藏族寺院及被列为怀疑对象的藏人家中频繁进行“突袭搜查”，故而其亦成为被当局因政治原因而维稳、监控的打击对象；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被阿坝县警方从僧舍中强行带走，并被关押在远离阿坝县的一家看守所内，另有格尔登寺僧人洛桑塔克及阿坝河支寺僧人图巴亦被先后抓捕，自此失联；之后不久，其被阿坝县警方以不具名罪由转正式逮捕，被指控因其曾经“向境外发送文字消息”，故而属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，其案在甘孜藏族自治州阿坝县法院开庭审理，后被一审以不详罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。目前被羁押于四川省阿坝县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑格培（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">现年<span lang="EN-US">29</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县麦尔玛乡第二大队人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，曾因政治诉求于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被当局抓捕并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被提前数月释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被警方突然从其僧舍带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。据悉，其直到一个月前仍处于下落不明状态，且当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑嘉扬（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省阿坝自治州阿坝县僧人，现年<span lang="EN-US">28</span>岁，笔名为“鲁米”的藏人作家，是阿坝县麦尔玛乡第三村人。嘉杨自小在阿坝格德寺出家为僧，几年前遭中共当局从该寺驱逐后，前往色达喇荣五明佛学院等佛教寺院继续修学佛法。因在著作中自由表达观点便于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月遭逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日家人获悉他在两个月前被中共当局指控“泄露国家机密”与“分裂国家”罪非法判处了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半有期徒刑。洛桑嘉杨告诉前去探视的亲属，他从未做过触犯法律的事情，也从未向当局“承认”过什么罪行。现在汶川县某监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑克珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">现年<span lang="EN-US">44</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县贾柯河牧场人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾因政治诉求被当局抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后因当时在狱中受虐严重，导致罹患重病而被提前释放，后经由家人、亲友自筹经费，让其住院长时治疗，才得以转危为安。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被警方突然从其僧舍带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其因被指控涉嫌“在微信建立组群为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿，特别收集长寿祈愿文持诵及持咒数量”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑曲达（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏安多阿坝县格德寺僧人。中共当局最初在阿坝等地开展“爱国爱教”运动时，他就曾表达不满，并在县政府前张贴文字进行抗议，当时被判处了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年徒刑。出狱后于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年参与当地的和平抗议活动，呼喊出达赖喇嘛返回西藏的诉求，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被中共警方再次抓捕，约一年后被阿坝县中级人民法院指控“煽动分裂国家”、“代领民众开展示威”，遭判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，现在四川省绵阳监狱中服刑，近日获悉其身体健康状况出现严重问题。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑桑杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，青海省果洛州久治县人，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺（又译格德寺）僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因向外透露格尔登寺僧人自焚抗议事件真相，而被中共当地警方抓捕、刑拘，后被转正式逮捕，并被追加指控涉嫌制作、出售达赖喇嘛的相片和讲法的影片等，违法了中国法律，遂于当年被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日秘密获释；据悉，其在狱中因遭受酷刑虐待，以致出狱时身体状况极差，出现丧失记忆症状；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其再次被当地警方以涉嫌藏人自焚抗议等“政治问题”抓捕、刑拘；在非法关押长达<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月之后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院一审以“政治问题”（不知名罪名）重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日；因当地对藏族群体高压严控情况十分严重，故其具体情况缺详。目前其羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑坦凯（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿坝县格尔登寺僧人。他<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁。他自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，也是曾被中国当局关闭的寺属学校“佛学青年文苑”第三届毕业生，被捕前在格尔登寺辩经学院中观班就读。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被捕，具体日期不详。洛桑坦凯于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被当局判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。除此之外，有关他被指控的罪名、被关押的地点等情况，因为当局过度的言行限制及网络审查而无法进一步了解。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛桑西热（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">现年<span lang="EN-US">36</span>岁，四川省阿坝羌族藏族自治州若尔盖县唐克镇俄色村人，索克藏寺续部学院僧人和寺院商店管理员。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夜里，在自己僧舍里突遭一批不属于当地警方的国保警察野蛮抓捕。抓捕之时，不仅不说明理由，而且还使用暴力，用手铐铐住双手，用枪顶住脸部，将其弄伤。此后长期失联，官方拒绝透露其被捕原因、关押地点及其身体状况等信息。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被四川阿坝羌族藏族自治州黑水县法院以“煽动分裂国家”、“非法联系境外”罪秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前关押地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洛珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：现年<span lang="EN-US">41</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县安斗乡克洼村人，当地知名画家东阔之子，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因政治诉求而被当局抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被警方带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月下旬。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗保军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗翠琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州毕节威宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因发放法轮功资料挂横幅，朱家彩、罗翠琴遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在毕节七星关区法院被庭审，后得知朱家彩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款二万元、罗翠琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款一万元。罗翠琴刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗春泉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省梅州市兴宁市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，罗春泉遭国保警察绑架，梅州市兴宁市国保大队到罗春泉家，没有出示搜查证，却乱翻东西，抢走电脑、打印机、书籍等。国保罗织黑材料，已将罗春泉构陷到检察院。罗春泉已被关押在看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗兰青：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，湖北襄阳市樊城警方协助河北大冶警方在樊城区某酒店抓获湖北网络大<span lang="EN-US">V</span>罗兰青。后罗被大冶警方带回，予以刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日罗兰青终获和父亲会见，会见后其父罗兆义发视频介绍说儿子面色黄瘦、神情恍惚，狱中境况堪忧，疑遭酷刑殴打。罗兰青长期关注民生社会问题，才遭到当局通缉抓捕的。罗兰青一直为弱势群体呐喊，敢于揭露抨击腐败。他在微博上长期关注环保话题，曾因举报劲牌酒厂污染环境等问题，多年不敢归家。被抓的是网络大<span lang="EN-US">V</span>罗兰青，微博拥有近<span lang="EN-US">19</span>万粉丝，他的微博更新时间定格在<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">19:15</span>分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗丽：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，辽阳法轮功学员李伟涛、王永生、国世游、谷林杰、汤显贺、罗丽被辽阳市白塔公安分局国保警察马文博等人绑架、抄家，当时国世游身体不适被多个警察抬着抓走的。辽宁省辽阳市白塔区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月对李伟涛等六名法轮功学员判刑，刑期是：李伟涛<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王永生<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罗丽<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、汤显贺<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、国世游<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、谷林杰<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并附带罚款，其中五人已上诉。罗丽刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗让才让（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，四川省阿坝县牧民。中共当局指控其叔叔罗让贡求长期与境外藏独组织“格尔底寺新闻联络小组”成员三木旦保持密切联系，罗让贡求单独或者同其侄子罗让才让一起鼓动自焚并将自焚信息提供给三木旦，一些境外媒体利用这些信息进行分裂主义宣传。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日罗让才让被四川警察抓走，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日四川阿坝中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处罗让才让有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗让贡求（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，四川省阿坝县格尔登寺僧人；中共当局指控罗让贡求长期与境外藏独组织“格尔底寺新闻联络小组”成员三木旦保持密切联系，罗让贡求单独或者同其侄子罗让才让一起鼓动自焚并将自焚信息提供给三木旦，一些境外媒体利用这些信息进行分裂主义宣传。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日罗让贡求被四川警察抓走，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日四川阿坝中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处罗让贡求死缓，剥夺政治权利终身。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">骆雪梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川古蔺县古蔺镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，法轮功学员周糢珍和骆雪梅在习水县醒民镇钢铁村，告诉百姓法轮功真相，被举报。醒民镇派出所抓捕了周糢珍和骆雪梅<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，周糢珍和骆雪梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕耿松：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，浙江省杭州市人，前浙江省高等公安专科学校教师，独立撰稿人，中国民主党浙江委员会重要成员，人权活动家，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日因言获罪被抄家拘捕，并被羁押于浙江省杭州市西湖看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被杭州市中级人民法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日刑满获释。出狱后因仍持守民主理念，关注民主宪政建设，帮助访民维权，遂遭到中共当局严密监控和恶意打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被杭州市警方抄家、传唤；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被杭州市警方以涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被杭州市检察院转正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被杭州市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬经浙江省杭州市高级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。目前在浙江省湖州市长湖监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕国妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕国妹是上海浦东新区唐镇前进村西李家宅<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号吕湘福的女儿，他家的合法私有房屋在家庭人员坚守在屋顶护家园抗强拆<span lang="EN-US">6</span>天<span lang="EN-US">5</span>夜半，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">12</span>时许被中共政府强拆。参与护家园抗强拆的今年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁的吕湘福，<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚上被警察带走，同时被带走的另外<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名屋顶抗争者都下落不明。后吕国妹的家属收到《拘留通知书》才知道吕国妹已于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日<span lang="EN-US">19</span>：<span lang="EN-US">55</span>分被上海市公安局浦东分局以“拒不执行判决罪”为名刑事拘留，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕三秀</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁，江西省樟树市人，原江西省宜春市樟树市冶炼厂职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功曾遭当局非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、前后劳教两次、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，累计共系狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，惨遭酷刑、下毒等折磨，一度曾被迫害致疯。释放回家后，当局为达到控制她的目的，一直不给她补办社保金和身份证，令其基本生活无法维持。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因其在樟树市义城乡宣传法轮功，于是被当地派出所警察再次抓捕，并被拘留于樟树市看守所，二十多天后，又被转押到宜春市看守所予以刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，其已被当局枉法构陷，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕淑玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南宝丰县南关镇访民。因为和邻居的伤害纠纷报警后，警方对她造成了<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次伤害，此后吕淑玲就开始上访维权导致被拘留了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，吕淑玲在北京正常上访时，南关派出所<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多个人赶到北京直接拿着传唤证把她从北京带回来以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，羁押在宝丰县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕月霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕月霞与赵文静、黄金桔、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><br /></div>
